         <p data-reactid="3215">Reverting to using .npmignore, the "files" syntax forgot the knex.js file</p>
        </div>
        <div data-reactid="3216">
         <b class="header" data-reactid="3217">0.6.0</b>
         <!-- react-text: 3218 --> — 
         <!-- /react-text -->
         <small data-reactid="3219"><i data-reactid="3220">June 4, 2014</i></small>
         <br data-reactid="3221">
         <b data-reactid="3222">Major Library refactor:</b>
         <ul data-reactid="3223">
          <li data-reactid="3224">Major internal overhaul to clean up the various dialect code.</li>
          <li data-reactid="3225">Improved unit test suite.</li>
          <li data-reactid="3226">Support for the <a href="https://github.com/mscdex/node-mariasql">mariasql</a> driver.</li>
          <li data-reactid="3227">More consistent use of raw query bindings throughout the library.</li>
          <li data-reactid="3228">Queries are more composable, may be injected in various points throughout the builder.</li>
          <li data-reactid="3229">Added <a href="#Interfaces-Streams">streaming</a> interface</li>
          <li data-reactid="3230">Deprecated 5 argument <a href="#Builder-join">join</a> in favor of additional join methods.</li>
          <li data-reactid="3231">The wrapValue function to allow for array column operations in PostgreSQL (<a href="https://github.com/tgriesser/knex/issues/287">#287</a>).</li>
          <li data-reactid="3232">An explicit connection can be passed for any query (<a href="https://github.com/tgriesser/knex/issues/56">#56</a>).</li>
          <li data-reactid="3233">Drop column support for sqlite3</li>
          <li data-reactid="3234">All schema actions are run sequentially on the same connection if chained.</li>
          <li data-reactid="3235">Schema actions can now be wrapped in a transaction</li>
          <li data-reactid="3236"><code>.references(tableName.columnName)</code> as shorthand for <code>.references(columnName).inTable(tableName)</code></li>
          <li data-reactid="3237"><code>.join('table.column', 'otherTable.column')</code> as shorthand for .join('table.column', '=', 'otherTable.column')</li>
          <li data-reactid="3238">Streams are supported for selects, passing through to the streaming capabilities of node-mysql and node-postgres</li>
          <li data-reactid="3239">For More information, see this <a href="https://github.com/tgriesser/knex/pull/252">pull-request</a></li>
         </ul>
        </div>
        <div data-reactid="3240">

         <small data-reactid="3348"><i data-reactid="3349">Dec 12, 2013</i></small>
         <br data-reactid="3350">
         <ul data-reactid="3351">
          <li data-reactid="3352">The <a href="#Builder-returning">returning</a> in PostgreSQL may now accept * or an array of columns to return.           <li data-reactid="3353">Added <code>bigint</code> and <code>bigserial</code> type to PostgreSQL. (<a href="https://github.com/tgriesser/knex/issues/111">#111</a>)</li>

          <li data-reactid="3355">Several fixes for migrations, including migration file path fixes, passing a Promise constructor to the migration <code>up</code> and <code>down</code> methods, allowing the "knex" module to be used globally, file ordering on migrations, and other small improvements.         <div data-reactid="3468">
         <b class="header" data-reactid="3469">0.4.0</b>
         <!-- react-text: 3470 --> — 
         <!-- /react-text -->
         <small data-reactid="3471"><i data-reactid="3472">Sep 13, 2013</i></small>
         <br data-reactid="3473">
         <b data-reactid="3474">Breaking Changes:</b>
         <ul data-reactid="3475">
          <li data-reactid="3476">Global state is no longer stored in the library, an instance is returned from <code>Knex.initialize</code>, so you will need to call this once and then reference this <code>knex</code> client elsewhere in your application.</li>
          <li data-reactid="3477">Lowercasing of <code>knex.raw</code>, <code>knex.transaction</code>, and <code>knex.schema</code>.</li>
          <li data-reactid="3478">Created columns are now nullable by default, unless <code>notNullable</code> is chained as an option.</li>
          <li data-reactid="3479">Keys created with <code>increments</code> are now assumed to be unsigned (MySQL) by default.</li>
          <li data-reactid="3480">The <code>destroyAllNow</code> is no longer called by the library on <code>process.exit</code> event. If you need to call it explicitly yourself, you may use <code>knex.client.destroyPool</code></li>
         </ul>
        </div>

         <small data-reactid="3526"><i data-reactid="3527">Aug 7, 2013</i></small>
         <br data-reactid="3528">
         <b data-reactid="3529">Breaking changes:</b>
         <ul data-reactid="3530">
          <li data-reactid="3531"><a href="#Schema-hasTable">hasTable</a> now returns a boolean rather than a failed promise.</li>
          <li data-reactid="3532">Changed syntax for insert in postgresql, where the <code>id</code> is not assumed on inserts (<a href="https://github.com/tgriesser/knex/issues/18">#18</a>). The second parameter of <a href="#Builder-insert">insert</a> is now required to return an array of insert id's for the last insert.</li>
          <li data-reactid="3533">The <a href="#Schema-timestamp">timestamp</a> method on the schema builder now uses a <code>dateTime</code> rather than a <code>timestamp</code></li>
         </ul>
        </div>
